 com / ofp4jvphiu The Delhi High Court on Wednesday demanded the city police commissioner to know why Urdu or Persian words are being used in the FIR (FIR), while the complainants do not use them
 saath hi, adaalat ne kaha ki praathmiki main baari-bharkam shabdon ke bajaay saamaanya bhashaa kaa istemaal kiya janaa chahie
 a bench of Chief Justice DN Patel and Justice c Hari Shankar told the Delhi Police that the FIR should be in the words of the complainant and should not be used in 'lexical language', which means searching in the dictionary
 adaalat ne kaha ki police aam aadmi kaa kaam karne ke liye he, sirf un logon ke liye nahin he jinke paas urdu yaa farsi main doctoret kii degree he
 The bench told the Delhi Police, "very lenient language, which has to be found in the dictionary, should not be used
 exiaar shikayatakarta ke shabdon main honi chahie
 (FIR) Easy language should be used instead of heavy word
 logon ko jaananaa hota he ki kya likhaa gaya he
 This also applies to the use of English
 baari bharkam shabdon kaa istemaal nahin karen
 "the court has filed an affidavit to the Commissioner of Police to clarify whether the agency (police) is used by the urdu-persian or the complainants

 Mahashivratri is a very auspicious and big festival for Hindus
 bhole baba ko prasann karne ke liye is din bhakt khub dhoomdhaam se ye tyohaar manaate hai
 According to Hindu belief, Mahashivaratri is celebrated in the 11th month of the Hindi calendar
 is din ko ' shiv kii mahaan raatri' ke rup main bhi janaa jaataa he
 It is said that Lord Shiva saved the earth from being destroyed on this day
 unhone ye shart bhi rakhi thi, ki sabhi bhakt unki sachhee shraddha se puja or upasna karen
 Though there are many more beliefs and beliefs, but today we tell you how to please Bhole Baba so that this Maha Shivaratri will be auspicious for your family
 bhagwaan shiv ko prasann karne ke liye un par ye 10 chije arpit zarur karen-1
 Milk- Anointing of Bhole Baba with milk is considered very virtuous
 doodh arpit karne se vyakti sadaiv swasth or rog mukt rahata he
 According to Vishnupuran, during the churning of the ocean, Shiva had ingested all the poison in his throat, due to which his whole body started turning blue
 tab sabhi devataaon ne unka doodh se abhishek kiya or vish kaa asar un par kam ho gaya
 Since then, milk is very dear to Lord Shiva
 2
 Water- If you offer water on the Shivling while chanting 'om Namah Shivaya', your mind will be calm and you will feel compassion
 manyata ke anusaar vish kaa prabhaav kam karne ke liye devataaon ne unke upar jal daalaa tha
 Since then, he was decorated with the name of Neelkanth
 3
 Sugar is also offered on the Shiva lingam on the occasion of chini-mahashivratri
 is paavan avasar par bhole baba ko chini arpan karnaa laabhadaayak he
 It will never lack fame, glory and fame in your home and their blessings will always remain
 4
 Saffron: Tilak of Lord Shiva with red saffron brings mildness in life and ends Manglik Dosh
 aisa kehete he ki mahashivaratri par agar apane vyapaarik dastavejon par kesar se tilak karenge, to sabhi adchane dur hongi or dhandha kabhi manda nahin padegaa
 5
 itr- shivlinga par itr chhidakna shubh mana gaya he
 Perfume spraying purifies our mind and we are able to be free from tamasic tendencies
 bhole baba par itr chhidakane se bhakton ko sadbuddhi milti he or wo kabhi bhi satya kii raah se nahi bhatakate
 6
 dahi- shiv ji ko dahi chadhaane se vyakti paripakv banataa he or uske jivan main sthirataa aati he
 It is also believed that if Bhole Baba is offered yogurt regularly, then all the obstacles and difficulties of life are removed
 7
 Ghee - Desi Ghee is a symbol of strength
 isliye shivlinga par ghi se abhishek karne se vyakti balavaan banataa he
 Offer Ghee to Lord Shiva to get children
 aisa karne se ghar main bachche kii kilkaari avashya guunjegi
 8
 chandan- veda puraanon ke mutabik mahakaal ko chandan lagane se ek insaan ko aakarshak rup miltaa he or uske jivan main maan, sammaan or khyaati kii kabhi kami nahin aati 
 9
